How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Boots
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Feet
- Color: Blue
- Stat Buffs
    - Movement Speed ✦ = Lx1.5
    - Armor ✦ = L÷2
    - Defense DC = L÷3
- Actives:
    - [Protect Ally](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Protect+Ally)
    - You have access to Tiers I-II your Active.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Ydilikian (Medieval)
